  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/199276500" />
    <a title="t&#39;irla ~The Bookslayer~ aka Barbara" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5601870-t-irla-the-bookslayer-aka-barbara"><img alt="t&#39;irla ~The Bookslayer~ aka Barbara" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1507934269p2/5601870.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/199276500?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="t&#39;irla ~The Bookslayer~ aka Barbara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="t&#39;irla ~The Bookslayer~ aka Barbara" href="/user/show/5601870-t-irla-the-bookslayer-aka-barbara">t&#39;irla ~The Bookslayer~ aka Barbara</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone how enjoys humor, vampires and dentists</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to t'irla ~The Bookslayer~ by: </span>
      PA Lupton, Enabler extrodinaire 
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5601870-t-irla-the-bookslayer-aka-barbara?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5601870-t-irla-the-bookslayer-aka-barbara?shelf=4-star-read">4-star-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer199276500" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer680858783384118778">On the run from the Russian Mob Shanna finds herself protected by a vampire lord. She also finds herself hunted by a vampire lord. Can things get worse, yup they can..she falls in love with her vampire lord...well she doesn't know he is a vampire at first...worst of all...her father is not a diplomat....<br/><br/>My first Kerrelyn Sparks novel and I must say I LOVED it! Her characters are funny, quirky and completely lovable. The reach out of the pages and grab you. She writes from both her heroine's POV </span>
  <span id="freeText680858783384118778" style="display:none">On the run from the Russian Mob Shanna finds herself protected by a vampire lord. She also finds herself hunted by a vampire lord. Can things get worse, yup they can..she falls in love with her vampire lord...well she doesn't know he is a vampire at first...worst of all...her father is not a diplomat....<br /><br />My first Kerrelyn Sparks novel and I must say I LOVED it! Her characters are funny, quirky and completely lovable. The reach out of the pages and grab you. She writes from both her heroine's POV but also from some of the other characters pov as well. Like Roman's our hero's...full of angst yet still domineering in all the right ways. His harem is side splitting funny and his sidekicks are just so delicious. I can't wait to read their stories. I'm still shaking my head smiling, a vampire who looses a fang and needs a dentist...looses it in a blowup doll....you just have to read this book.<br /><br />A strong 4 star rating from me...and I can't wait for the next book.<br /><br />Reread: Listened on Audiobook Dec 2012/Jan 2013 Loved the narrator she did awesome voices and I'm still in love with the story. Currently listening to book 2 and it is even better. <br /><br />I will say again a book and a series not to be ignored!</span>
  <a data-text-id="680858783384118778" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IDdGpH1dIAZdp/roJezFS7I1GK+c5fLwSwARUMyZnxmPO2hx3wq7zMxsGM9esjv/LKRH2f45lksm0tgA3ht+Cw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('QX1ydEg8/oTJIhxnj/+iFtRuranD/UvxAl0UmqJKWOXucVyh6mtlTljp/kD0oVyiSv/y36EhL0pvj93KsMi59w==')})
  }
//]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer15985614695164619585">Kerrelyn Sparks apparently has issues with reality. After writing more than a dozen books about vampires, she has now completely gone off the deep end and wound up on another planet. But how thrilling that she can share this magical new world with her readers! Although she is best known (so far) for the Love at Stake series, which has hit as high as number 5 on the New York Times list and 22 on th</span>
  <span id="freeText15985614695164619585" style="display:none">Kerrelyn Sparks apparently has issues with reality. After writing more than a dozen books about vampires, she has now completely gone off the deep end and wound up on another planet. But how thrilling that she can share this magical new world with her readers! Although she is best known (so far) for the Love at Stake series, which has hit as high as number 5 on the New York Times list and 22 on the USA Today list, she hopes her readers will love The Embraced as much as they did her merry band of vamps and shifters. To learn more about her paranormal, historical, and upcoming out-of-this-world fantasy romances, please visit Kerrelyn on Facebook, Twitter, or her website at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.kerrelynsparks.com">www.kerrelynsparks.com</a>.<br /><br />Kerrelyn loves hearing from readers, even those who howl at the moon. Letters may be sent to P.O. Box 5512, Katy, TX 77491-5512. If you would like bookmarks and signed bookplates, please mail a Self-Addressed Stamped Envelope to her P.O. Box, and she will send those items to you.<br /><br /></span>
